<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
Initially, the user confirmed a bug fix related to raw material stock financials was working. They then requested a new feature: a full procurement workflow for raw materials, similar to the existing Purchase Order (PO) and Goods Received Note (GRN) system for products, but without syncing to WooCommerce.

After the successful implementation of the Raw Material Procurement module, the user requested another major feature: a comprehensive **Payroll Module**.

**PRODUCT REQUIREMENTS (Payroll Module):**
*   **Employee Types:** Handle permanent staff, casual staff, freelancers, and others.
*   **Pay Structures:** Support fixed salaries and task-based payments.
*   **Core Components:**
    *   **Employee Management:** Onboarding/offboarding, personal details, roles, departments.
    *   **Attendance Tracking:** Manual entry for tracking work days/hours.
    *   **Leave Management:** System to apply for and approve leave.
    *   **Payroll Processing:** Automated calculation of salaries, deductions, overtime, and allowances.
    *   **Advances & Loans:** Track and deduct salary advances.
    *   **Financial Integration:** Automatically create journal entries for salaries, EPF/ETF, etc., in the financial system.
*   **Statutory Compliance (Sri Lanka):**
    *   **EPF:** 20% total contribution (12% employer, 8% employee).
    *   **ETF:** 3% employer contribution.
*   **Overtime:** Configurable rates (defaults: 1.25x for weekdays, 1.5x for weekends).
*   **Departments:** Manually created.
*   **Reporting:** Generate all necessary payroll reports (payslips, summary reports, statutory reports).

**User's preferred language**: English

**what currently exists?**
The application is a full-stack ERP system. In this session, a complete Raw Material (RM) Procurement module was added, including RM Suppliers, RM Purchase Orders, RM GRNs, and RM GRN Returns. This module is fully functional and tested.

Additionally, the basic scaffolding for a new **Payroll Module** has been created. This includes backend API routes and placeholder frontend pages for Departments, Employees, Salary Structure, Leave Management, Advances, and Reports. The navigation links and routes are set up, but the core business logic within these components is not yet implemented.
